<script>

//Funktion för att rensa text på otillåtna tecken
var conv = function (str) {
    if (!str) {
        str = 'empty';
    }  return str.replace(/[!\"#$%&'\(\)\*\+,\.\/:;<=>\?\@\[\\\]\^`\{\|\}~]/g, '')
              .replace(/ /g, "")
              .toLowerCase()
              .trim();
};

//Skapa lista med alla html element med klassen "example-item".
var catArray = document.querySelectorAll('.example-item');

//Lägg på rätt klasser och lägg i samlad div
catArray.forEach( function(elem) {
    var text_kategori = conv(elem.childNodes[1].innerText || elem.childNodes[1].innerContent);
    var text_tillverkare = conv(elem.childNodes[2].childNodes[0].innerText || elem.childNodes[2].childNodes[0].innerContent);
    var text_modell = conv(elem.childNodes[2].childNodes[1].innerText || elem.childNodes[2].childNodes[1].innerContent);
    elem.classList.add(text_tillverkare, text_modell, text_kategori);
    document.getElementsByClassName("examples-collection-list")[0].appendChild(elem);
});

//Ta bort de efterföljande tomma listorna
var wrappers = document.getElementsByClassName("examples-wrapper");
var wrappers_length = wrappers.length;
for (i = 1; i < wrappers_length; i++) {
  wrappers[1].remove();
}

// init Isotope GRID 1
var $grid1 = $('#grid1').isotope({
  itemSelector: '.example-item',
  layoutMode: 'fitRows',
});

//Use URL hash to filter
var hashFilter = decodeURIComponent(window.location.hash);
if( hashFilter ) {
  var hashFilter = "." + hashFilter.slice(1);
  $grid1.isotope({ filter: hashFilter });
}

// use value of search field to filter
var qsRegex;
var $quicksearch = $('#quicksearch').keyup( debounce( function() {
  qsRegex = new RegExp( $quicksearch.val().replace(/ /g, ""), 'gi' );
  $grid1.isotope({ filter: function() {
    return qsRegex ? $(this).text().replace(/ /g, "").match( qsRegex ) : true;
}})}, 200 ));

// debounce so filtering doesn't happen every millisecond
function debounce( fn, threshold ) {
  var timeout;
  threshold = threshold || 100;
  return function debounced() {
    clearTimeout( timeout );
    var args = arguments;
    var _this = this;
    function delayed() {
      fn.apply( _this, args );
    }
    timeout = setTimeout( delayed, threshold );
  };
}

//Knapp för att rensa fritext sök
$('#clear-qs').on( 'click', function() {
  document.getElementById("quicksearch").value = "";
  $grid1.isotope({ filter: '*'});
});

//Filtrering med kategorierna
$('.category-filter-wrapper').on( 'click', 'div', function() {
  var filterValue = $(this).attr('data-filter');
  $grid1.isotope({ filter: filterValue });
  window.location.hash = encodeURIComponent(filterValue.slice(1));

});

Webflow.push(function() {
  // Disable submitting form fields
  $('#quicksearch-wrapper-examples').submit(function() {
    return false;
  });
});

</script></body></html>
